# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 005 SOVIET COLLAPSE EFFECTS
# ============================================================================
# This file owns the clean Soviet Collapse crisis scaffold: opening pressure
# setup, breakaway support, crisis-meter arithmetic, and the Soviet objective
# board activation queue. Event stages use these effects; evolutions remain
# separate mutation tracks and are not represented here as stage logs.
# ============================================================================

@soviet_collapse_ukr_bread_state_building_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_ukr_bread_state_fort_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_moldova_route_building_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_moldova_route_fort_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_central_asia_league_building_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_central_asia_league_fort_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_route_building_level = 1
@soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_route_resource_gain = 4

soviet_collapse_clamp_crisis_components = {
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
}

soviet_collapse_update_center_pressure_state = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_state
			must_soviet_collapse_exit_calm_strong_center_state = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_state }
			can_soviet_collapse_enter_calm_strong_center_state = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_state
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_dynamic_pressure_caps = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = yes }
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_republic_confidence_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_depot_vulnerability_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_foreign_appetite_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_league_cohesion_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_old_movement_cap }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
			}
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_republic_confidence_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_depot_vulnerability_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_foreign_appetite_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_league_cohesion_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_old_movement_cap }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_republic_confidence_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_depot_vulnerability_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_foreign_appetite_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_league_cohesion_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_old_movement_cap }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_republic_confidence_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_depot_vulnerability_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_appetite_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_league_cohesion_cap }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_old_movement_cap }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_monthly_component_growth_caps = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_republic_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_depot_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_league_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_old_movement_pressure }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_old_movement_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_republic_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_depot_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_league_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_old_movement_pressure }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_old_movement_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_republic_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_depot_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_league_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_old_movement_pressure }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_old_movement_component_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = soviet_collapse_component_growth_cap } }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_source_pressure_caps = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min compare = greater_than }
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			}
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_source_republic_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_source_depot_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_source_league_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = soviet_collapse_last_month_moscow_authority }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_source_authority_erosion_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor compare = less_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = soviet_collapse_last_month_military_obedience }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_source_obedience_erosion_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor compare = less_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min compare = greater_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_source_republic_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_source_depot_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_source_league_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = soviet_collapse_last_month_moscow_authority }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_source_authority_erosion_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor compare = less_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = soviet_collapse_last_month_military_obedience }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_source_obedience_erosion_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor compare = less_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min compare = greater_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_source_republic_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_source_depot_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_source_league_month_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap compare = greater_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = soviet_collapse_last_month_moscow_authority }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_source_authority_erosion_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor compare = less_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = soviet_collapse_last_month_military_obedience }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_source_obedience_erosion_cap }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor compare = less_than } } set_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor } }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_cap = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_source_floor = 0 }
}

soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = {
	soviet_collapse_clamp_crisis_components = yes
	soviet_collapse_update_center_pressure_state = yes
	soviet_collapse_apply_dynamic_pressure_caps = yes
	soviet_collapse_apply_monthly_component_growth_caps = yes
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_source_pressure_caps = yes
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_offset }
	subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority }
	subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_military_obedience }
	multiply_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_multiplier }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening value = 0 compare = greater_than }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening }
	}
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
			is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_first_month_total_ceiling
				compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_first_month_total_ceiling }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = yes }
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_total_ceiling
				compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_total_ceiling }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_total_threat_ceiling
				compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_total_threat_ceiling }
	}
	soviet_collapse_apply_timeout_burst_pressure_caps = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired }
		}
		soviet_collapse_maybe_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_timeout_burst_pressure_caps = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.timeout_burst_failure_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.chaos_tier_5_failed_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.chaos_tier_4_failed_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.war_failed_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_failed_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_failed_month_cap }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap value = 0 compare = greater_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_delta = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_delta = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_delta value = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap compare = greater_than }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_over_cap = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_delta }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_over_cap = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening value = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_over_cap compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_over_cap }
			}
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap }
			clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling }
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_cap = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_delta = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_timeout_burst_threat_over_cap = 0 }
}

soviet_collapse_register_monthly_threat_success = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives = 1 }
}

soviet_collapse_register_monthly_threat_failure = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives = 1 }
}

soviet_collapse_decay_progressive_release_pressure = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_soviet_collapse_calm_release_recovery_window = yes
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min compare = greater_than }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_release_pressure_decay }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
			min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
			max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_cap
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta value = 0 compare = greater_than }
		}
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
					is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
				}
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_month_cap compare = greater_than }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_month_cap }
			subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_month_cap compare = greater_than }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_month_cap }
			subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_month_cap compare = greater_than }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_month_cap }
			subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_month_cap compare = greater_than }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_month_cap }
			subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_over_cap }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_month_cap }
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta value = 0 compare = less_than }
		}
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = 0 }
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_patron_pressure_delta = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta value = 0 compare = greater_than }
		}
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
					is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
				}
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = greater_than }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_patron_month_cap }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap }
			clamp_temp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta min = 0 max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_patron_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = greater_than }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_patron_month_cap }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap }
			clamp_temp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta min = 0 max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_patron_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = greater_than }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_patron_month_cap }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap }
			clamp_temp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta min = 0 max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_patron_month_cap }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = greater_than }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_patron_month_cap }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_pressure_over_cap }
			clamp_temp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta min = 0 max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
			set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_patron_month_cap }
		}
	}
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
}

soviet_collapse_set_monthly_threat_guard_cap = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_over_cap = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_over_cap = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_over_cap = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_over_cap
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling
	}
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_over_cap }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap }
	clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_floor max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling }
}

soviet_collapse_apply_monthly_success_recovery = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_soviet_collapse_calm_release_recovery_window = yes
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.success_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = less_than }
		}
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_authority_recovery }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_obedience_recovery }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_republic_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_depot_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_foreign_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_league_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_old_movement_relief }
		soviet_collapse_clamp_crisis_components = yes
		soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.success_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_authority_recovery }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_obedience_recovery }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_republic_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_depot_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_foreign_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_league_relief }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_old_movement_relief }
		soviet_collapse_clamp_crisis_components = yes
		soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_update_terminal_pacing = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_soviet_collapse_active = yes }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_months_active = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat
					compare = greater_than
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.min_breakaways_for_union_unmade
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_contested_authority
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
					has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months = 1 }
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months
			min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
			max = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_pressure_months_cap
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_monthly_threat_guard = {
	soviet_collapse_update_center_pressure_state = yes
	soviet_collapse_apply_monthly_success_recovery = yes
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat }

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.success_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_month_cap compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_success_month_cap }
		soviet_collapse_set_monthly_threat_guard_cap = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
			}
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_failed_month_cap compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_failed_month_cap }
		soviet_collapse_set_monthly_threat_guard_cap = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.success_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion compare = less_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_month_cap compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_success_month_cap }
		soviet_collapse_set_monthly_threat_guard_cap = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_delta value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_failed_month_cap compare = greater_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_failed_month_cap }
		soviet_collapse_set_monthly_threat_guard_cap = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening = 0 }
	}

	soviet_collapse_update_terminal_pacing = yes
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_military_obedience = soviet_collapse_military_obedience }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_old_movement_pressure = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_successful_objectives = soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_timeout_aid_grants = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_cap = 0 }
}

	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_support_equipment_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.support_equipment_req }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_train_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.train_req }

	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_manpower_req = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.manpower_req }
}

soviet_collapse_initialize_crisis_values = {
	set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_active
	set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_first_month_lock_days = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.first_month_lock_days }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
				days = [FIRST_MONTH_LOCK_DAYS]
			}
		}
		FIRST_MONTH_LOCK_DAYS = "[?soviet_collapse_first_month_lock_days|.0]"
	}
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_center
	add_ideas = soviet_collapse_union_crisis

	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.moscow_authority }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.republic_confidence }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.military_obedience }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.depot_vulnerability }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.old_movement_pressure }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_military_obedience = soviet_collapse_military_obedience }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_old_movement_pressure = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_months_active = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months = 0 }
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics

	soviet_collapse_initialize_mission_requirements = yes
	refresh_world_threat_state = yes
	count_fired_major_events = yes
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_current_event_id = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.event_id }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { major_events_count > 0 }
			is_in_array = { global.fired_events = soviet_collapse_current_event_id }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { major_events_count = 1 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { major_events_count > 0 } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_prior_major_event_confidence = major_events_count }
		multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_prior_major_event_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.prior_major_event_republic_confidence }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_prior_major_event_confidence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_prior_major_event_authority = major_events_count }
		multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_prior_major_event_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.prior_major_event_authority }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_prior_major_event_authority }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = world_in_threat }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_world_threat_authority }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_world_threat_obedience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_world_threat_foreign_appetite }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_world_threat_sources = global.world_threat_source_count }
		multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_world_threat_sources = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_world_threat_source_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_active_world_threat_sources }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 1 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_1 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_2 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_2 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_2_foreign_appetite }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_3_old_movement_pressure }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4 }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_4_old_movement_pressure }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final_foreign_appetite }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.chaos_tier_final_old_movement_pressure }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_stability < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_stability }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_stability }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_stability_authority }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_war_support < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_war_support }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_war_support_obedience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.low_war_support }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_war }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.active_war }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { capital_scope = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } } }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.capital_lost_authority }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.capital_lost }
	}

	soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_moscow_authority = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_military_obedience = soviet_collapse_military_obedience }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_republic_confidence = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_depot_vulnerability = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_foreign_appetite = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_league_cohesion = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_old_movement_pressure = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_successful_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_timeout_aid_grants = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_successful_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_pressure = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_monthly_threat_dampening = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_months_active = 0 }
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months = 0 }
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.129 days = 30 }
}

soviet_collapse_apply_successful_authority_objective_pressure = {
	soviet_collapse_register_monthly_threat_success = yes
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = constant:soviet_collapse_objective_pressure.authority_success_authority }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_objective_pressure.authority_success_confidence }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_objective_pressure.authority_success_foreign }
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
	soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
}

	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
	soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.10 days = 1 }
}

soviet_collapse_spawn_loyalist_militias = {
	division_template = {
		name = "Emergency Loyalist Militia"
		is_locked = yes
		force_allow_recruiting = yes
		regiments = {
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
			infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_loyalist_militia_count = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.loyalist_militia_unit_count }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Emergency Loyalist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
					owner = PREV
					count = [UNIT_COUNT]
				}
			}
		}
		UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_loyalist_militia_count|.0]"
	}
}

soviet_collapse_emit_super_event = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = super_event_visible
				days = 30
				value = [SUPER_EVENT_ID]
			}
		}
		SUPER_EVENT_ID = "[?soviet_collapse_super_event_id|.0]"
	}
	set_variable = { global.current_super_event_audio_id = soviet_collapse_super_event_id }
	every_country = {
		limit = { is_ai = no }
		play_current_super_event_audio = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_show_union_unmade_super_event = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired } }
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
			SOV = { soviet_collapse_apply_terminal_collapse = yes }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_super_event_id = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade }
		soviet_collapse_emit_super_event = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_maybe_show_union_unmade_super_event = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_super_event_union_unmade_fired }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock }
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.min_breakaways_for_union_unmade
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat
						compare = greater_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_critical_authority
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_contested_authority
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat
						compare = greater_than
					}
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
						has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_first_wave_failed
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.deep_collapse_threat
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_terminal_ordinary_republics = {
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			exists = no
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = BLR
				tag = KAZ
				tag = MOL
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
				tag = GEO
				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
				tag = UZB
				tag = KYR
				tag = TAJ
				tag = TMS
				tag = KAR
				tag = KOM
				tag = CRI
				tag = TAT
				tag = BSK
				tag = FER
				tag = YAK
				tag = BYA
				tag = TAN
			}
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = PREV
				is_owned_by = SOV
				is_controlled_by = SOV
			}
		}
		SOV = { release = PREV }
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
			}
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject_of = SOV
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = BLR
				tag = KAZ
				tag = MOL
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
				tag = GEO
				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
				tag = UZB
				tag = KYR
				tag = TAJ
				tag = TMS
				tag = KAR
				tag = KOM
				tag = CRI
				tag = TAT
				tag = BSK
				tag = FER
				tag = YAK
				tag = BYA
				tag = TAN
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		}
		SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_subject_freed_report_pending
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
		soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			tag = KAZ
			has_soviet_collapse_three_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					exists = no
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_owned_by = SOV
						is_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = no }
			SOV = { release = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
			set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_subject_freed_report_pending
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_prepare_highest_chaos_terminal_successors = {
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_sailor_assembly_voted
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_huliaipole_quiet_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_basmachi_supply_chain_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_tashkent_anchor_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_first_wave_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_loyal_military_districts_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_union_archives_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_ural_factory_gates_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_peasant_anger_joined_green_army
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_villages_negotiation_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_mountain_administration_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_vladivostok_buffer_government_credible
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_siberian_distance_command_failed
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_ural_workers_directorate_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mountain_republic_council_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_idel_ural_league_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_birobidzhan_commune_declared
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_northern_port_directorate_declared
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_old_movement_pressure_high
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_old_movement_pressure_high }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_spawn_terminal_high_chaos_successors = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.spawn_old_movement_pressure_gate
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_prepare_highest_chaos_terminal_successors = yes
	}
	soviet_collapse_maybe_spawn_high_chaos_successors = yes
}

soviet_collapse_form_terminal_leagues = {
	soviet_collapse_form_terminal_regional_leagues = yes
	soviet_collapse_form_terminal_free_republics_league = yes
}

soviet_collapse_join_terminal_anti_soviet_war = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			can_declare_war_on = SOV
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SOV
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_start_terminal_anti_soviet_war = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
			NOT = { tag = SOV }
		}
		soviet_collapse_join_terminal_anti_soviet_war = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_terminal_collapse = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse } }
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse_in_progress
		soviet_collapse_release_terminal_ordinary_republics = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_subject_freed_report_pending }
			country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.46 }
			clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_subject_freed_report_pending
		}
		soviet_collapse_spawn_terminal_high_chaos_successors = yes
		soviet_collapse_form_terminal_leagues = yes
		soviet_collapse_start_terminal_anti_soviet_war = yes
		soviet_collapse_cleanup_terminal_collapse_missions = yes
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse
		clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse_in_progress
		soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
	}
}
