soviet_collapse_cleanup_resolved_breakaway_target = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		remove_from_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
		add_to_variable = { global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { var = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.any_breakaway_count compare = less_than } }
			set_variable = { global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.any_breakaway_count }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = -1 }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.any_breakaway_count compare = less_than } }
					set_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.any_breakaway_count }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_corridor_open
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_protection_treaty_signed
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_adviser_privileges_granted
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_client_cabinet_installed
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_warning
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_lock
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_protection_treaty_sponsor_germany
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_protection_treaty_sponsor_japan
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_protection_treaty_sponsor_italy
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_adviser_privileges_sponsor_germany
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_adviser_privileges_sponsor_japan
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_adviser_privileges_sponsor_italy
	if = { limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } } SOV = { soviet_collapse_prune_invalid_active_soviet_objectives = yes } }

soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_setup_package = {
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway

		array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries
		value = THIS
	}
	add_to_variable = { global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_count = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active }
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_breakaway_republic_confidence }
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_breakaway_depot_vulnerability }

				soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
					PREV = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes }
				}
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_major_republic_confidence }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
					PREV = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes }
				}
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_opening_pressure.first_wave_regional_republic_confidence }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active }
				soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
			}
			soviet_collapse_maybe_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
		}
	}

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_breakaway_manpower_package = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.base_manpower }

			}
			FIELD_UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_breakaway_field_unit_count|.0]"
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_internal_republic_news_reported }
			OR = {
				tag = KAR
				tag = KOM
				tag = CRI
				tag = TAT
				tag = BSK
				tag = FER
				tag = YAK
				tag = BYA
				tag = TAN
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_internal_republic_news_reported
		news_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.95 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_dynamic_unit_report_seen }
		}
		set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_dynamic_unit_report_seen
		SOV = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.47 days = 1 } }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_check_republic_recovery = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.partial_recovery
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder
			add_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_republic_startup_disorder_mitigated
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder
				has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.recovery_complete
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder } remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated } remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_republican_startup_disorder_mitigated }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_emergency_administration_stabilized
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.institution_decision_gain }
		soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_republic_startup_disorder_resolved
	}
}

soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.decision_progress }
	soviet_collapse_check_republic_recovery = yes
}

soviet_collapse_add_republic_focus_recovery_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_recovery_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_recovery.focus_progress }
	soviet_collapse_check_republic_recovery = yes
}

soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_recognition_request = {
	add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.recognition_stability_spend
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.recognition_progress }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.institution_decision_gain }
	soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
	soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.recognition_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.recognition_soviet_republic_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_mobilization = {
	add_political_power = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.mobilize_political_power_spend
	add_command_power = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.mobilize_command_power_spend
	add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.mobilize_manpower
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.mobilize_infantry_equipment }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.military_focus_gain }
	soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
	soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_mobilize_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.mobilize_unit_count }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Emergency Republican Guard\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.85"
					owner = PREV
					count = [UNIT_COUNT]
				}
			}
		}
		UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_mobilize_unit_count|.0]"
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_breakaway_front_coordination = {
	add_fuel = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_fuel_spend
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_support_equipment_spend }
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
			}
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_support_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.league_gain }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_recognition_progress }
			soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
			soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }

			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.coordinate_league_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = {
	FROM = {
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_total = soviet_collapse_influence_delta }
	}
	if = { limit = { tag = GER } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_germany = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = ENG } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_britain = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = JAP } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_japan = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = FRA } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_france = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = USA } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_usa = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = TUR } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_turkey = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = PER } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_iran = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = POL } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_poland = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = ROM } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_romania = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = FIN } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_finland = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = SWE } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_sweden = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	if = { limit = { tag = ITA } FROM = { add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_italy = soviet_collapse_influence_delta } } }
	FROM = { soviet_collapse_update_sponsor_balance_pressure = yes }
}

soviet_collapse_update_sponsor_balance_pressure = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_germany value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_germany value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_germany }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_germany value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_germany }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_britain value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}

		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_britain value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_britain }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_britain value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_britain }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_japan value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }

		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_usa }

		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_turkey }

		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_poland }

		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_romania value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_romania }

		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_romania }
	}
	if = {

		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_finland value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_finland }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_finland value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_finland }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_sweden value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_sweden value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_sweden }

	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_sweden value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_sweden }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_italy value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_sponsor_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_italy value = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_italy }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_italy value = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence compare = greater_than } }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence = soviet_collapse_influence_italy }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap = soviet_collapse_second_foreign_sponsor_influence }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count value = 3 compare = less_than }
		}
		clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_three_resilience_remove }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_three_patronage_risk_remove }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count value = 2 compare = less_than }
		}
		clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_two_resilience_remove }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_two_patronage_risk_remove }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_two_resilience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_two_patronage_risk }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_three_resilience }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.balanced_three_patronage_risk }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_warning }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_influence compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_gap compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_warning
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_patronage_risk }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_warning_resilience }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_lock }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_top_foreign_sponsor_influence value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_influence compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_gap value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_gap compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_lock
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_patronage_risk }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.dominant_lock_resilience }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
		clamp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max }
	}
}

	soviet_collapse_clear_republic_staged_ideas = yes
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_support_strength = soviet_collapse_influence_total }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_strength_bonus = soviet_collapse_active_foreign_sponsor_count }
	multiply_temp_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_strength_bonus value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.foreign_sponsor_stage_bonus }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_support_strength = soviet_collapse_foreign_sponsor_strength_bonus }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_material_support_strength = soviet_collapse_influence_arms_total }
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_material_support_strength = soviet_collapse_influence_logistics_total }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.stage_4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		add_ideas = soviet_collapse_republic_institutions_4
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.stage_3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }

soviet_collapse_reduce_republic_league_support = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_republic_league_coordination = yes }
		subtract_from_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_support_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.league_gain }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_league_support_strength
			min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
			max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max
		}
		soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = {
	soviet_collapse_update_sponsor_balance_pressure = yes
	soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_recognition_aid = {
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_democratic_patron_contest_completed }
	if = { limit = { has_war_with = SOV } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_hostile_patron_double_game }
	add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_stability_spend
	add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_war_support_spend
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_regional_stability_extra_spend
		add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_regional_war_support_extra_spend
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_major_stability_extra_spend
		add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_major_war_support_extra_spend
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.recognition_influence }
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = yes
	FROM = {
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_general_aid_recipient = yes
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_progress }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_recognition_total = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.recognition_influence }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.institution_decision_gain }
		soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
		soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_recognition_news_reported } }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_recognition_news_reported
			news_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.49 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_patron_pressure_delta = yes
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.recognition_soviet_republic_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_liaison_aid = {
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_democratic_patron_contest_completed }
	if = { limit = { has_war_with = SOV } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_hostile_patron_double_game }
	add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_stability_spend
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_regional_stability_extra_spend
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes } }
		add_stability = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_major_stability_extra_spend
	}
	if = { limit = { has_government = communism } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	if = { limit = { has_government = fascism } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	if = { limit = { has_government = neutrality } FROM = { add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_ideology_popularity } } }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.liaison_ideology_influence }
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = yes
	FROM = {
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_general_aid_recipient = yes
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_recognition_progress }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_ideology_total = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.liaison_ideology_influence }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.liaison_patronage_risk }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.institution_decision_gain }
		soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
		soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.liaison_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_patron_pressure_delta = yes
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_armaments_aid = {
	if = { limit = { has_war_with = SOV } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_hostile_patron_double_game }
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_infantry_equipment_spend }
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_support_equipment_spend }
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes } }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_regional_infantry_equipment_extra_spend }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_regional_support_equipment_extra_spend }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes } }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_major_infantry_equipment_extra_spend }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_major_support_equipment_extra_spend }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.armaments_arms_influence }
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = yes
	FROM = {
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_general_aid_recipient = yes
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_major_aid_recipient = yes
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_target_infantry_equipment producer = ROOT }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_target_support_equipment producer = ROOT }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_control = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.armaments_depot_control }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_arms_total = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.armaments_arms_influence }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_logistics_total = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.armaments_logistics_influence }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.depot_focus_gain }
		soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
		soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }

soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_volunteer_aid = {
	if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_democratic_patron_contest_completed }
	if = { limit = { has_war_with = SOV } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_hostile_patron_double_game }
	add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_manpower_spend
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_infantry_equipment_spend }
	transfer_units_fraction = {
		target = FROM
		target_organization = 1
		source_organization = 1
		size = 0
		stockpile_ratio = 0
		army_ratio = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_army_transfer_fraction
		navy_ratio = 0
		air_ratio = 0
		keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = yes } }
		add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_regional_manpower_extra_spend
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_regional_infantry_equipment_extra_spend }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes } }
		add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_major_manpower_extra_spend
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_major_infantry_equipment_extra_spend }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.volunteers_influence }
	soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_influence_delta = yes
	FROM = {
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_general_aid_recipient = yes
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_major_aid_recipient = yes
		soviet_collapse_mark_foreign_volunteer_aid_recipient = yes
		add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_target_manpower
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_target_infantry_equipment producer = ROOT }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_volunteer_unit_count = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_target_unit_count }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Emergency Republican Field Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.9"
						owner = PREV
						count = [VOLUNTEER_UNIT_COUNT]
					}
				}
			}
			VOLUNTEER_UNIT_COUNT = "[?soviet_collapse_foreign_volunteer_unit_count|.0]"
		}
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_recognition_progress }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_volunteers_total = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.volunteers_influence }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.volunteers_patronage_risk }
		soviet_collapse_add_republic_decision_recovery_progress = yes
		soviet_collapse_update_foreign_investment_stage_ideas = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_patron_pressure_delta = yes
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.volunteers_soviet_republic_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
}

ukr_soviet_collapse_apply_bread_state_soviet_pressure = {
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = ukr_soviet_collapse_bread_state_old_movement_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = constant:soviet_collapse_ukraine_bread_state.soviet_depot_pressure }
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_ukraine_bread_state.soviet_foreign_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { ukr_soviet_collapse_bread_state_old_movement_pressure = 0 }
}

		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability = mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_depot_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_league_pressure }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure = mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_old_movement_pressure }
			set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_foreign_pressure }
			soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_depot_pressure = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_league_pressure = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_old_movement_pressure = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { mol_soviet_collapse_route_soviet_foreign_pressure = 0 }
}

	add_state_claim = 834

		limit = {
			CRI = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			NOT = { has_war_with = CRI }
			can_declare_war_on = CRI
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = CRI
			expire = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				controls_state = 137
			}
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			can_declare_war_on = SOV
		}
		create_wargoal = {

		}
	}
}

	if = { limit = { 834 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT is_claimed_by = ROOT NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } } } 834 = { add_core_of = ROOT } }

	if = { limit = { 93 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT is_claimed_by = ROOT NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } } } 93 = { add_core_of = ROOT } }

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			tag = BLR
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_belarus_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			tag = KAZ
		}

				tag = EST

				tag = ARM
				tag = AZR
			}

				tag = TAJ

		}

	}

		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = soviet_collapse_internal_republic_focus_tree }
	}
	if = {

		}

			limit = {

soviet_collapse_maybe_report_single_republic_liaison_office = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_single_republic_liaison_reported }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = { tag = LIT tag = LAT tag = EST }
					has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_member_ready = yes
					NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_quorum = yes }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = { tag = GEO tag = ARM tag = AZR }
					has_soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_member_ready = yes
					NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_quorum = yes }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = { tag = UZB tag = KYR tag = TAJ tag = TMS tag = KAZ }
					has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_member_ready = yes
					NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_single_republic_liaison_reported
		country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.45 }
	}
}

		}
	}

soviet_collapse_refresh_baltic_regional_faction = {
	if = { limit = { LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_founder } } LIT = { soviet_collapse_invite_baltic_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { LAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_founder } } LAT = { soviet_collapse_invite_baltic_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { EST = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_founder } } EST = { soviet_collapse_invite_baltic_regional_partners = yes } }
}

soviet_collapse_refresh_caucasus_regional_faction = {
	if = { limit = { GEO = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_founder } } GEO = { soviet_collapse_invite_caucasus_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { ARM = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_founder } } ARM = { soviet_collapse_invite_caucasus_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { AZR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_founder } } AZR = { soviet_collapse_invite_caucasus_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { MRC = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_founder } } MRC = { soviet_collapse_invite_caucasus_regional_partners = yes } }
}

soviet_collapse_refresh_central_asian_regional_faction = {
	if = { limit = { UZB = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } UZB = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { KYR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } KYR = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { TAJ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } TAJ = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { TMS = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } TMS = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } KAZ = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { BSC = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } BSC = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { TNC = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } TNC = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
	else_if = { limit = { ALA = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_founder } } ALA = { soviet_collapse_invite_central_asian_regional_partners = yes } }
}

soviet_collapse_form_terminal_regional_leagues = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_quorum = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_announced }
		}
		if = { limit = { LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } LIT = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_baltic_restoration_pact = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { LAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } LAT = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_baltic_restoration_pact = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { EST = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } EST = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_baltic_restoration_pact = yes } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_announced }
		soviet_collapse_refresh_baltic_regional_faction = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_quorum = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_announced }
		}
		if = { limit = { GEO = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } GEO = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_caucasus_defense_compact = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { ARM = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } ARM = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_caucasus_defense_compact = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { AZR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } AZR = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_caucasus_defense_compact = yes } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_announced }
		soviet_collapse_refresh_caucasus_regional_faction = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_announced }
		}
		if = { limit = { UZB = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } UZB = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_central_asian_league = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { KYR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } KYR = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_central_asian_league = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { TAJ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } TAJ = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_central_asian_league = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { TMS = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } TMS = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_central_asian_league = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } KAZ = { soviet_collapse_found_terminal_central_asian_league = yes } }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_announced }
		soviet_collapse_refresh_central_asian_regional_faction = yes
	}
}

	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_defense_goal
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recognition_goal
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_logistics_goal
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_goal_cooldown_days = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_resolution_cooldown_days }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_recently_resolved
				days = [GOAL_COOLDOWN_DAYS]
			}
		}
		GOAL_COOLDOWN_DAYS = "[?soviet_collapse_regional_goal_cooldown_days|.0]"
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_regional_faction_goal_success = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_defense_goal }
		add_war_support = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.war_support_small
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member = yes }
			add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_manpower_reward
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_equipment_reward }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recognition_goal }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.recognition_goal_gain }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_success_resilience }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_logistics_goal }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_depot_control = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.depot_gain }
		add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.emergency_manpower
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.medium_infantry_equipment }
	}
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_success_recorded
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_faction_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_success_cohesion }
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_faction_tension = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_success_tension }
	every_other_country = {
		limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member = yes }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_independence_resilience = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.resilience_gain }
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_support_strength = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_idea.league_gain }
		soviet_collapse_update_consolidated_republic_ideas = yes
	}
	soviet_collapse_clear_regional_faction_goal = yes
	soviet_collapse_apply_regional_faction_soviet_pressure = yes
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.41 }
}

		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }

		}
	}
	soviet_collapse_clear_regional_faction_goal = yes
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.42 }
}

soviet_collapse_maybe_resolve_regional_faction_goal = {

		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_success = yes }
		soviet_collapse_apply_regional_faction_goal_success = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_failure = yes }
		soviet_collapse_apply_regional_faction_goal_failure = yes
	}
}

soviet_collapse_withdraw_from_regional_faction = {
	set_country_flag = { flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recently_left days = 180 }
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_member
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_member
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_member
	remove_ideas = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_commitments
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_recognition_progress = -1 }
	if = { limit = { is_in_faction = yes } leave_faction = yes }
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.44 }
}

soviet_collapse_call_regional_league_defensive_war = {
	add_command_power = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_command_power_spend
	add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_manpower_spend
	set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_league_defensive_war_called
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			can_declare_war_on = SOV
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SOV
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member = yes
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
		}
		add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_manpower_reward
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.war_equipment_reward }
		add_to_war = {
			targeted_alliance = ROOT
			enemy = SOV
			hostility_reason = asked_to_join
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes } }
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_league_cohesion = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.soviet_release_pressure }
				add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.soviet_release_pressure }
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_foreign_pressure_delta = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.soviet_foreign_pressure }
				soviet_collapse_apply_foreign_pressure_delta = yes
				soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
			}
		}
	soviet_collapse_maybe_resolve_regional_faction_goal = yes
	country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.43 }
}

		else_if = { limit = { KOM = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } KOM = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { TAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } TAT = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { BSK = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } BSK = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { CRI = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } CRI = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { FER = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } FER = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { YAK = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway is_in_faction = no } } YAK = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }

		else_if = { limit = { SZA = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor is_in_faction = no } } SZA = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { FEV = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor is_in_faction = no } } FEV = { soviet_collapse_form_free_republics_league_from_ukraine = yes } }

	}

soviet_collapse_record_high_chaos_successor_evolution = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_event_id = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.event_id }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.evolution_type }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.totalen_tier }
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.world_collapse_tier }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { can_soviet_collapse_record_high_chaos_evolution_this_tier = yes }
		save_event_target_as = events_log_evolution_actor
		record_events_log_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
			set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_evolution_tier_5_recorded
		}
		else = {
			set_global_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_evolution_tier_4_recorded
		}
	}
}

		state = 248
		remember_old_capital = no
	}
	soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
	load_focus_tree = { tree = CFR_soviet_collapse_focus_tree keep_completed = no }
	set_variable = { cfr_construction_mandates = constant:soviet_collapse_factory_ancient.medium_mandate_gain }
	add_ideas = cfr_construction_mandates
	add_ideas = cfr_housing_ration_boards

soviet_collapse_spawn_cfr_if_enabled = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_event_id = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.event_id }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.evolution_type }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:soviet_collapse_high_chaos_event_log.civilian_factory_stage }
	if = {
		limit = {
			can_soviet_collapse_spawn_cfr = yes
			is_current_evolution_enabled = yes
		}
		248 = {
			add_core_of = CFR
			transfer_state_to = CFR
		}
		253 = {
			add_core_of = CFR
			transfer_state_to = CFR
		}
		CFR = { soviet_collapse_setup_cfr_successor = yes }

soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_western_republic = {
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = BLR
				tag = MOL
				tag = LIT
				tag = LAT
				tag = EST
			}
			NOT = { is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS } }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					exists = no
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_owned_by = SOV
						is_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				AND = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		random_select_amount = 1
		add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_add_regional_priority_progressive_republic = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_two_western_republics_free = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
				is_soviet_collapse_western_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_quorum = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
				is_soviet_collapse_baltic_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_quorum = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
				is_soviet_collapse_caucasus_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes
			}
		}
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
				is_soviet_collapse_central_asian_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes
			}
		}
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
				is_soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_internal_release_cascade_pressure = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
				is_soviet_collapse_internal_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_add_random_threat_breakaway_republic = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
		soviet_collapse_add_regional_priority_progressive_republic = yes
	}
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected } }
			is_soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate = yes
		}
		random_select_amount = 1
		SOV = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
		add_to_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection value = THIS }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_save_regional_priority_progressive_republic_target = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_two_western_republics_free = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
				is_soviet_collapse_western_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			save_event_target_as = soviet_collapse_release_target
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_quorum = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
				is_soviet_collapse_baltic_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			save_event_target_as = soviet_collapse_release_target
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_quorum = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
				is_soviet_collapse_caucasus_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			save_event_target_as = soviet_collapse_release_target
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes
			}
		}
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
				is_soviet_collapse_central_asian_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			save_event_target_as = soviet_collapse_release_target
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes
			}
		}
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
				is_soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			save_event_target_as = soviet_collapse_release_target
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_internal_release_cascade_pressure = yes }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
				is_soviet_collapse_internal_progressive_release_candidate = yes
			}
			random_select_amount = 1
			save_event_target_as = soviet_collapse_release_target
		}
	}
}
