soviet_collapse_count_progressive_release_candidates = {
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count = 0 }
	every_possible_country = {
		limit = {
			is_soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate = yes
		}
		SOV = {
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count = 1 }
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_release_regional_cascade = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score = 0 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_western_republics_free = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_quorum = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_per_active_region_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_quorum = yes
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_per_active_region_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_quorum = yes
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_per_active_region_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_soviet_collapse_internal_release_cascade_pressure = yes
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_per_active_region_add }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_release_pressure_gain = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_monthly_add }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.urgency_pressure_per_score }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.urgency_pressure_monthly_cap
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_pressure_per_score }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_pressure_monthly_cap
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_pressure_per_candidate }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_pressure_monthly_cap
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			NOT = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.high_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.moderate_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.high_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			NOT = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.high_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			NOT = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.critical_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.severe_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.critical_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.critical_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = less_than }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.weak_authority_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = less_than }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.weak_obedience_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_soviet_collapse_failure_release_pressure = yes }
		add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.failure_pressure_monthly_add }
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_monthly_gain_cap
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_component = 0 }
}

soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_candidate_release_weight = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_count_weight_add }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
			}
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_count_calm_cap }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.high_threat compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_count_moderate_cap }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_count_high_cap }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_count_terminal_cap }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight value = soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight = soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap }
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.candidate_count_weight_cap
	}
}

soviet_collapse_apply_progressive_release_final_weight_dampening = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.moscow_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.military_obedience compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.high_authority_factor }
		multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.high_obedience_factor }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = less_than }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.opening_strong_center_release_factor }
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.miss_weight_ceiling
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_event_target_progressive_republic = {
	event_target:soviet_collapse_release_target = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = no }
			SOV = { release = PREV }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_finish_progressive_release = {
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown_days = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.cooldown_days }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown
				days = [COOLDOWN_DAYS]
			}
		}
		COOLDOWN_DAYS = "[?soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown_days|.0]"
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_one_threat_breakaway_republic = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target } }
		clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection
		clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected
		soviet_collapse_add_random_threat_breakaway_republic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
		soviet_collapse_release_event_target_progressive_republic = yes
		soviet_collapse_finish_progressive_release = yes
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_selected }
			soviet_collapse_release_selected_progressive_republics = yes
			soviet_collapse_finish_progressive_release = yes
		}
		else = {
			clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_fire_progressive_release_event = {
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_ministry_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_ministry_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_rail_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_rail_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_border_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_border_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_party_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_party_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_foreign_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_foreign_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_depot_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_depot_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_old_movement_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_old_movement_weight }
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_league_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.cause_league_weight }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_foreign_weight = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.depot_vulnerability compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_depot_weight = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.old_movement_pressure compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_old_movement_weight = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_league_pressure_ready = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion compare = less_than_or_equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_cause_league_weight = 0 }
	}
	soviet_collapse_save_random_threat_breakaway_republic_target = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target }
		random_list = {
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_ministry_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.130 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_rail_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.131 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_border_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.132 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_party_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.133 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_foreign_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.134 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_depot_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.135 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_old_movement_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.136 } }
			var:soviet_collapse_release_cause_league_weight = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr5.137 } }
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_release_urgency = {
	set_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = 0 }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.republic_confidence }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.momentum_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.momentum_per_point_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.moscow_authority }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.authority_deficit_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.authority_deficit_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.military_obedience }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_military_obedience }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_max
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.obedience_deficit_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.obedience_deficit_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.low_threat }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.threat_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.threat_per_point_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.foreign_appetite }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.foreign_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.foreign_per_point_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.depot_vulnerability }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.depot_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.depot_per_point_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.league_cohesion }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.league_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.league_per_point_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.old_movement_pressure }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.old_movement_per_point_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.old_movement_per_point_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_breakaway_gate }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.breakaway_count_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.breakaway_count_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives }
	multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.last_failed_objective_add }
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.last_failed_objective_cap
	}
	add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component }

	clamp_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score
		min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
		max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.release_urgency_cap
	}
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_component = 0 }
}

soviet_collapse_accumulate_progressive_release_pressure = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pacing_ready = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_real_release_pressure = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_compound_release_pressure = yes
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count value = 0 compare = greater_than }
		}
		soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_release_pressure_gain = yes
		add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
			min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
			max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_cap
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure_gain = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_release_pressure = yes }
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_compound_release_pressure = yes }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure = 0 }
	}
}

soviet_collapse_maybe_release_threat_breakaway = {
	soviet_collapse_count_progressive_release_candidates = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count value = 0 compare = greater_than }
		}
		soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_release_urgency = yes
		soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_release_regional_cascade = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score = 0 }
	}
	soviet_collapse_decay_progressive_release_pressure = yes
	soviet_collapse_accumulate_progressive_release_pressure = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				can_soviet_collapse_roll_progressive_release = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_accumulated_release_pressure = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.total_threat_ceiling
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			soviet_collapse_maybe_show_union_unmade_super_event = yes
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count value = 0 compare = greater_than }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = mtth:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight }
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = mtth:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight }
				soviet_collapse_compute_progressive_candidate_release_weight = yes
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_weight = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score }
				multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_release_urgency_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.release_urgency_weight_factor }
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_weight
					min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
					max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.release_urgency_weight_cap
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight }
				add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure }
				add_to_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_weight }
				soviet_collapse_apply_progressive_release_final_weight_dampening = yes
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction = soviet_collapse_regional_cascade_score }
				multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_miss_reduction_per_score }
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction
					min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
					max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.regional_cascade_miss_reduction_cap
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction }
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score }
				multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.urgency_miss_reduction_per_score }
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction
					min = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.component_min
					max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.urgency_miss_reduction_cap
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction }
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight
					min = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.miss_weight_floor
					max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.miss_weight_ceiling
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_miss_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					}
					multiply_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_miss_factor }
				}
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight
					min = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.miss_weight_floor
					max = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.miss_weight_ceiling
				}
				random_list = {
					var:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_weight = { soviet_collapse_fire_progressive_release_event = yes }
					var:soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_weight = { }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_candidate_weight_cap = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_miss_reduction = 0 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_selected_first_wave_republics = {
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics
		if = {
			limit = { exists = no }
			SOV = { release = PREV }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_selected_progressive_republics = {
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.soviet_collapse_progressive_release_selection
		if = {
			limit = { exists = no }
			SOV = { release = PREV }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free } }
			set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = yes }
			soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes
			soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_release_initial_republics = {
	clear_array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics

	soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_western_republic = yes
	soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_caucasus_republic = yes
	soviet_collapse_add_random_first_wave_central_asian_republic = yes

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				AND = {
					has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
					OR = {
						has_stability < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_stability
						has_war_support < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.good_war_support
					}
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_add_random_extra_first_wave_republic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
				AND = {
					has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
					has_stability < constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.min_stability
				}
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_add_random_extra_first_wave_republic = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		soviet_collapse_add_random_extra_first_wave_republic = yes
	}

	soviet_collapse_release_selected_first_wave_republics = yes

	if = {
		limit = { can_soviet_collapse_open_kazakhstan_first_wave = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { KAZ = { exists = no } }
			release = KAZ
			KAZ = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV } }
			set_autonomy = { target = KAZ autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			KAZ = { set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			KAZ = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			}
		}
		KAZ = { soviet_collapse_setup_breakaway_country = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_southern_breakaway_active = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = { UZB = { exists = no } }
				release = UZB
				UZB = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UZB = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV } }
				set_autonomy = { target = UZB autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
				UZB = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					}
					KYR = { exists = no }
				}
				release = KYR
				KYR = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					}
					KYR = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV }
				}
				set_autonomy = { target = KYR autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
				KYR = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					}
					TAJ = { exists = no }
				}
				release = TAJ
				TAJ = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
						has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					}
					TAJ = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV }
				}
				set_autonomy = { target = TAJ autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
				TAJ = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					TMS = { exists = no }
				}
				release = TMS
				TMS = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
					TMS = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SOV }
				}
				set_autonomy = { target = TMS autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
				TMS = { soviet_collapse_setup_southern_republic_if_valid = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	if = { limit = { UKR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } UKR = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { BLR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } BLR = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } KAZ = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { UZB = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } UZB = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { KYR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } KYR = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { TAJ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } TAJ = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	if = { limit = { TMS = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic } } TMS = { soviet_collapse_load_event_created_focus_tree = yes } }
	clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
}

soviet_collapse_cleanup_terminal_collapse_missions = {
	clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_active
	clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_wave_active
	clr_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_next_declaration_unarmed
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_next_declaration_armed
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_loyal_units_moved
	clr_country_flag = soviet_collapse_district_war_rooms_reopened
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objectives = 0 }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_001_confirm_the_emergency_chain_of_command } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_001_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_001_confirm_the_emergency_chain_of_command }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_002_seal_the_first_circular } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_002_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_002_seal_the_first_circular }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_003_guard_the_peoples_commissariats } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_003_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_003_guard_the_peoples_commissariats }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_004_establish_the_crisis_desk } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_004_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_004_establish_the_crisis_desk }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_005_count_the_missing_trains } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_005_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_005_count_the_missing_trains }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_006_freeze_unapproved_transfers } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_006_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_006_freeze_unapproved_transfers }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_007_order_the_border_posts_to_report_twice } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_007_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_007_order_the_border_posts_to_report_twice }
	if = { limit = { has_active_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_008_audit_the_republic_radios } set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_mission_008_done remove_mission = soviet_collapse_soviet_mission_008_audit_the_republic_radios }

soviet_collapse_queue_objective_refill = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_objective_refill_queued }
		}
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_objective_refill_queued
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_objective_refill_delay_days = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.objective_refill_delay_days }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				country_event = {
					id = chaosx.nr5.128
					days = [OBJECTIVE_REFILL_DAYS]
				}
			}
			OBJECTIVE_REFILL_DAYS = "[?soviet_collapse_objective_refill_delay_days|.0]"
		}
	}
}

soviet_collapse_activate_opening_objectives = {
	soviet_collapse_update_center_pressure_state = yes
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_objective_activation_grace } }
		set_country_flag = soviet_collapse_objective_activation_grace
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_objective_activation_grace_days = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.objective_activation_grace_days }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				country_event = {
					id = chaosx.nr5.127
					days = [OBJECTIVE_GRACE_DAYS]
				}
			}
			OBJECTIVE_GRACE_DAYS = "[?soviet_collapse_objective_activation_grace_days|.0]"
		}
	}
	soviet_collapse_prune_invalid_active_soviet_objectives = yes
	soviet_collapse_count_active_soviet_objectives = yes
	set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objective_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.active_cap }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objective_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.calm_active_cap }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes }
			is_soviet_collapse_calm_release_recovery_window = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objective_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.recovery_active_cap }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_calm_release_recovery_window = yes }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objective_cap = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_active_cap }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
		set_temp_variable = { soviet_collapse_active_objectives = soviet_collapse_active_objective_cap }
	}
	soviet_collapse_prune_surplus_active_soviet_objectives = yes
